The 0-vector.

  <a id="2729" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4239" class="Function Operator">∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Scaling by 0 gives the 0-vector.

Vector addition is commutative.

Vector addition is associative.

Scaling by a sum gives the sum of the scalings.

Scaling a sum gives the sum of the scalings.

    <a id="6343" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#2338" class="Function">0s</a>
  <a id="6348" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4239" class="Function Operator">∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Adding a row of 0s to the end of the matrix and then multiplying by a vector produces a vector with a 0 at the bottom.

Linear maps preserve scaling.

Multiplying by a standard basis vector projects out the corresponding column of the matrix.

The standard basis vectors put together give the identity matrix.

Extend a matrix as the identity matrix -- add a zero to the end of every row, and add a new row with a 1 and the rest 0s.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="extm"></a><a id="13221" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#13221" class="Function">extm</a> <a id="13226" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13228" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="13230" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13231" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#13231" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="13233" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#13233" class="Bound">δ</a><a id="13234" class="Symbol">}</a>

  <a id="13239" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13241" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#5473" class="Function">Matrix</a> <a id="13248" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#13231" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="13250" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#13233" class="Bound">δ</a>
    <a id="13256" class="Comment">--------------------------------</a>
